 routing bfd ip-sh sessions required-min-echo-tx-interval 10000
 routing bgp 66131
  address-family ipv4 unicast redistribute static
  multi-paths external 1
  multi-paths internal 1
  neighbor 172.30.85.66
   peer-type              external
   shutdown               false
   advertisement-interval 20
   update-source interface cre:bgp_lb_gtp
   bfd-enabled            false
   remote-asn             65055
   address-family ipv4 unicast
  !
  neighbor 172.30.85.67
   peer-type              external

epg pgw user-plane-pool pool DATA-pool
 node-name UPF55
  weight   1
  priority 1
 !
 node-name UPF65
  weight   1
  priority 1
 !
!
epg pgw user-plane-pool pool HDV-pool
 node-name UPF155
  weight   1
  priority 1
 !
!
epg pgw user-plane-selection intermediate-upf-enabled false
epg pgw user-plane-selection frame-pool-based-selection false
epg pgw user-plane-selection default-pool DATA-pool
epg pgw user-plane-selection selection-condition HDV
 data-network  [ ims ims-ipsec sos ]
 selected-pool HDV-pool
!
epg pgw user-plane-selection selection-condition DATA
 data-network  [ 5g-internet.sktelecom.com 5g.sktelecom.com lte.sktelecom.com smartport.sktelecom.com teenager.sktelecom.com tethering.sktelecom.com ]
 selected-pool DATA-pool
!
epg pgw control-plane signaling preservation-information
epg pgw control-plane signaling allow-invalid-gtp-restart-counter-msg false
epg pgw interface sx logical-interface sxb-cp-if
epg pgw interface sx heartbeat-interval 600
epg pgw interface sx association-interval 100
epg pgw interface sx graceful-release-interval 100
epg pgw interface sx n1   5
epg pgw interface sx t1   10
epg pgw interface sx no-pfcp-path-failure
epg pgw interface sx no-peer-restart
epg pgw interface sx diffserv af31
epg pgw interface sx heartbeat-times 1
epg pgw interface sx-u logical-interface sxb-cp-if
epg pgw interface sx-u diffserv af31
epg pgw interface s5s8-c logical-interface pgw-s5s8-c-if
epg pgw interface s5s8-c diffserv af31
epg pgw interface s5s8-c echo-interval-s 60.0
epg pgw interface s5s8-c n3-requests 3
epg pgw interface s5s8-c no-path-failure
epg pgw interface s5s8-c no-peer-restart
epg pgw interface s5s8-c t3-response-time-s 3.0
epg pgw interface s5s8-c transaction-timeout-s 5.0
epg pgw interface s5s8-c identify-sender-by-source-address
epg pgw interface s5s8-c no-path-management-for-peer address 0.0.0.0/1
!
epg pgw interface s5s8-c no-path-management-for-peer address 128.0.0.0/1
!
epg pgw logical-apn 5g-internet.sktelecom.com
 access-restrictions selection-mode public
 dnn-to-ue ue-requested
 apn default 5g-internet.sktelecom.com
 apn lzone-based-apn 44
  selected-apn teenager.sktelecom.com
 !
 apn lzone-based-apn 45
  selected-apn teenager.sktelecom.com
 !
 apn lzone-based-apn 46
  selected-apn smartport.sktelecom.com
 !
!
epg pgw logical-apn 5g.sktelecom.com
 access-restrictions selection-mode public
 dnn-to-ue ue-requested
 apn default 5g.sktelecom.com
 apn lzone-based-apn 44
  selected-apn teenager.sktelecom.com
 !
 apn lzone-based-apn 45
  selected-apn teenager.sktelecom.com
 !

epg pgw pdp-context limit          6600000
epg pgw pdp-context sgsn-rat-type gngp-handover keep-value
epg pgw pdp-context failover-back-off-timer value 5
epg pgw pdp-context failover-back-off-timer unit minute
epg pgw pdp-context host-route-limit 100000
epg pgw pdp-context allow-secondary
epg pgw pdp-context reject-request-without-valid-ue-id
epg pgw pdp-context session-control cause-code-in-manual-deletion
epg pgw pdp-context signaling session-creation-rate 8000
epg pgw pdp-context signaling locally-initiated-delete-rate 4800
epg pgw pdp-context signaling pfcp-modify-rate 100000
epg pgw policy-control gx-failure-profile DATA_EMER_Profile
 session-handling default-ccr-initial-failure-action CCRI_RM
 session-handling default-ccr-update-failure-action CCRU_RM
 session-handling connection-failure-action CCRU_RM
 session-handling action CCRI_RM
  continue local-policy-control profile DATA_EMER_LPC
 !
 session-handling action CCRU_RM
  continue retain
 !
!
epg pgw policy-control gx-failure-profile HDV_EMER_Profile
 session-handling default-ccr-initial-failure-action CCRI_RM
 session-handling default-ccr-update-failure-action CCRU_RM
 session-handling connection-failure-action CCRU_RM
 session-handling action CCRI_RM
  continue local-policy-control profile HDV_EMER_LPC
 !
 session-handling action CCRU_RM
  continue retain
 !
 pcc-rule-handling default-installation-failure-action Dedi_fail
 pcc-rule-handling default-modification-failure-action Dedi_fail
 pcc-rule-handling action Dedi_fail
  remove
  rule-failure-code 99
 !
!
epg pgw policy-control gx-profile DATA_PCF
 diameter-application-system       pcf
 subscription-id                   [ imsi msisdn ]
 always-include-ms-timezone
 always-include-plmn
 always-include-subscription-id
 always-include-user-location-info
 always-include-called-station-id
 always-include-rat-type
 qos-change-provisioning-required
 p-cscf-restoration-enhancement
 charging-control online enable
 ms-tz-in-raa-only-at-provision
 rai-in-raa-only-at-provision
 disable-gx-extensions
 monitoring-key encoding ascii
 access-network-charging-identifier encoding ascii
 pcc-release                       9
 select-apn                        requested
 failure-profile                   DATA_EMER_Profile
!

epg pgw policy-control local profile DATA_EMER_LPC
 unconditional pcc-rule-group [ NoQoS_NoGBR ]
 conditional action Quota_Expired
  pcc-rule-group [ OCS_Quota_Expired ]
 !
 conditional action WI_Denied
  pcc-rule-group [ WI_Denied ]
 !
 conditional condition cond_Qouta
  action                        Quota_Expired
  service-control-quota-expired active
 !
 conditional condition cond_WI
  action              WI_Denied
  service-control-odb active
 !
